a comprehensive chain of components spanning multiple files. The primary entry point is the CsrfViewMiddleware class in django/middleware/csrf.py, which validates incoming requests during the process_view method. The middleware uses a multi-layered approach: (1) Origin and Referer header verification via _origin_verified and _check_referer methods to validate request sources; (2) CSRF token validation via _check_token method which retrieves the CSRF secret using _get_secret; (3) Token format validation through _check_token_format to ensure proper length and character set. The critical token comparison is performed by _does_token_match function, which implements timing-attack protection by delegating to constant_time_compare from django/utils/crypto.py. This function uses Python's secrets.compare_digest for constant-time comparison, preventing attackers from inferring token validity through timing analysis. The token masking/unmasking mechanism is implemented via _mask_cipher_secret and _unmask_cipher_token functions to provide additional security layers. CSRF tokens are generated through get_token function and can be rotated via rotate_token. The middleware integrates with Django's decorator system in django/views/decorators/csrf.py, providing csrf_protect, requires_csrf_token, ensure_csrf_cookie, and csrf_exempt decorators as per-view alternatives to middleware-based protection. Template integration is handled through the csrf context processor in django/template/context_processors.py and the csrf_token template tag in django/template/defaulttags.py (CsrfTokenNode class), which renders hidden input fields containing the token. Failed CSRF validation triggers the csrf_failure view in django/views/csrf.py, which displays appropriate error messages to users attempting to bypass CSRF protection.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":10,"cache_creation_input_tokens":8081,"cache_read_input_tokens":55878,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":8081},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"5ef0db53-d7ab-4d35-86c8-d776011fbeed","uuid":"1e38e492-d9a7-45d8-8ace-7c5a3d52df4d"}

a comprehensive chain of components spanning multiple files. The primary entry point is the CsrfViewMiddleware class in django/middleware/csrf.py, which validates incoming requests during the process_view method. The middleware uses a multi-layered approach: (1) Origin and Referer header verification via _origin_verified and _check_referer methods to validate request sources; (2) CSRF token validation via _check_token method which retrieves the CSRF secret using _get_secret; (3) Token format validation through _check_token_format to ensure proper length and character set. The critical token comparison is performed by _does_token_match function, which implements timing-attack protection by delegating to constant_time_compare from django/utils/crypto.py. This function uses Python's secrets.compare_digest for constant-time comparison, preventing attackers from inferring token validity through timing analysis. The token masking/unmasking mechanism is implemented via _mask_cipher_secret and _unmask_cipher_token functions to provide additional security layers. CSRF tokens are generated through get_token function and can be rotated via rotate_token. The middleware integrates with Django's decorator system in django/views/decorators/csrf.py, providing csrf_protect, requires_csrf_token, ensure_csrf_cookie, and csrf_exempt decorators as per-view alternatives to middleware-based protection. Template integration is handled through the csrf context processor in django/template/context_processors.py and the csrf_token template tag in django/template/defaulttags.py (CsrfTokenNode class), which renders hidden input fields containing the token. Failed CSRF validation triggers the csrf_failure view in django/views/csrf.py, which displays appropriate error messages to users attempting to bypass CSRF protection.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
